So far AmericaOnDrugs has been a phenomenal vendor and I am Super excited to try my 1.5 ounces of penis envies and he surprised me with the strain of the half ounce of cannabis: God Bud!!! :)   

I'm an Extremely happy client and more than satisfied with AoD's customer service and flexibility and haven't even been able to actually place the custom order that AoD made for me yet until my coins are loaded tomorrow!  Keep your eyes peeled for the rest of the review when the order is purchased and when it gets here and is devoured!  - Communication / Customer Service:  Already off to a perfect start

Title: Re: AmericaOnDrugs: The Official Review Thread
Post by: norseman17 on May 12, 2013, 10:37 am
Thanks for the recognition AoD I try my best when it comes to giving good vendors the credit and recognition they deserve.. that being said my order got here already (Saturday morning) after ordering Thursday night across country so here's my review!!

Order: PE Cubensis + God's Gift Cannabis

Communication:  all I can say is perfect, nothing can be said negatively regarding AoD's customer service and response time for messages.  He not only responds rapidly with actual answers to what I ask without beating around the bush AND is willing to talk back and forth with me about any other questions I want to ask about future possibilities, products, custom stuff, what the weather is like... etc ya get the point!  Some (I'd venture to say most) vendors don't put this effort into customer service commonly using the excuse of being too busy which I totally get; but AoD sold out of ALL his bud and shrooms and EVERYTHING in like less than two days so I know he was super busy and he never said a thing about it.  As he says, he never sleeps and I believe it considering all the time spent catering to the client's every need!

Shipping: Fucking Ridiculously awesome and surprising.. ordered Thursday night, arrived Saturday morning regular priority mail.  The USPS says on their website for tracking that my order was scheduled to arrive until Monday and after I opened the package it (usps website) still said it was at the sorting facility hahaha AoD works wonders.. he must have an inside man in the post!  The stealth was excellent with all necessary measures taken and both the bud and cubes were packaged in a way that kept them pristine and not all smushed and compact (I hate when vendors do not take measures to prevent this) its not rocket science for those who squish their shit so any vendor who does this should order from AoD and take note Ha!

Appearance: 

PE Cubes - My first time having the opportunity to get some penis envy shrooms and I picked the right place.  Great looking quality; each fruit is intact and not all banged up and there was a cap for every stem!  Also there was no shake which is how it should be for an HQ item.  I once dosed 5+ grams of shake from a different vendor and had zero effect which meant it was probably just frickin' substrate powder I ate and was used to add weight to the order.. NOTE this was NOT AoD just saying this to show the significance of him giving me all whole shrooms!

God's Gift - I've ordered alot of great bud on the road so it's hard to blow me away but the smell alone did it for me... wait were not in that section yet.  The buds looked like top shelf should look.  Nice medium to large size I'd say .75 as the smallest to probably around 5g biggest which for the size of my order was amazing!  They nugs were covered in trichomes and nice and dense with many light orange hairs emerging from within the beautiful dark green buds!  The cure was perfect on the GG just enough resistance when broken apart by hand and sure to leave your fingers sticking together!

Smell/Taste

PE Cubes - smell like mushrooms, taste like mushrooms, they must be mushrooms! Hahah

God's Gift:  Godly is a good word to describe the smell and taste since the mirror each other perfectly.  This bud seriously REEKS of citrous like I just peeled a hundred oranges and limes and then a a super dank smell hits your nose and just stays there for a long time which is pleasant!

Potency:

I will update on the cubes since I haven't tried them yet but the cannabis gave me a really strong and instantaneous high which usually doesn't happen to me or hit me as hard since I consume large amounts of the plant.  This GG though was a different story and gave me a great head/mind high while leaving me able to function at my boss's dinner party which I attended right after sampling..  8)

AAA+  AmericaOnDrugs you did exactly what I predicted on Friday and Exceeded my expectations and for that I thank you!

 - N

Vendor: America On Drugs


Strain: Penuis Envy (mushrooms)

Package/Shipping:
   Awesome packaging, and shipping time :) Had perfect seals, and labeled digitally :) Only draw back would be the hand-placed
stamps for the postage. You can create a nice work flow for USPS by going digital, and it probably lessens number of times it has to be in route while in transit being shipped out.

Color/Appearance:
   Awesome thick specimens and really big :) The shrooms i got
where nice and thick, and very well colored, with its nice wrinkly off white stem, and blue trailing along the veins inward along the lining of the stem. The caps had a nice shape and very much looked
like what penises do, hence the name for it ! lol. Awesome coloring to the caps aswell, with about a 50/50 creamish brown/orangey gold color.
   

Image Link: http://xqz3u5drneuzhaeo.onion/users/qicpic/files/711.jpg

Smell/Aroma:
   That nice musky pscylocibe scent, thats drifts and can capture your nose, with a funky lil' stench that you can't deny :) Kinda like a fresh compost heap type of smelly.
   

Touch/Feel:
   The Shrooms where a nice bone dry feel and had no moisture in them, and where not like just picked fresh, no these where nice and
ready with a good feel of crunchiness and form.
   
   
Experience/Effect:
   I had ate the shrooms after around lunch time, and had planned to watch movies like "Dead Circles", and another one called "Warm Bodies", as i laid there waiting for my love to arrive, i had felt a slight lift of mood, as i got out the shower. The initial come up was not that intense compared to like golden teachers but i figured this was going to be less visual and more psychedelic then my previous experiences with mushrooms,but i was to be surprised. i had taken a bath and and finished within about 40 minutes into getting dressed i almost started forgetting my train of thought, as i appeared to stare at the floor now, thinking the floor that was like marble, had like juice stains on it, because i what i was seeing was the actual design of the marble floor and not like some old crummy strain of juice, what i had thought to be something was clearly not the case here. This is when i knew the shrooms were grooving in me, but like a silent creeper. I love this lil' moment where all time seems to stand still, and you can just feel like in a quiet head space of stillness and peace. By the time my significant other had arrived, i was with question on why and how, and what was i on ? I could feel, i was a lil' off, but the mushrooms where very controllable, and easy to maneuver in my normal functions, but it still had its own type of like leadway into perception and wonder, as i just kept it to myself among the questioning. :) By that time, i could see small morphs of colors and schemes from my perception, as i could see like colors kinda blend in endlessly and seemed to have like a nice warmer feel and a little more vibrant than when seeing things out of a clean sober eye. By this time, i was having a nice breakthrough and was easily able to communicate, and reflect off life so well, i had no problems expressing myself. I then got so much off my chest, and was able to get things done, all over the house, and still brought a new meaning to my life all awhile having a good time and enjoying myself. The initial onset, was sublime and didn't even leave a strong tummy feeling, this was really gentle as the come almost felt effortless, and non apparent, but soon i was to realize this strain is another league of its own when bringing the user its effects of goodness.Once my wave settled in, i was gone for a good strong hour and half, pretty much engulfed in my solitude and dependent on my imaginative adventure thinking. It was really introspective as i was able to start separating the difference of myself and how i project myself to others :) It took about a good or aswell to start subsiding and letting my vibe wear-off
   
Overall:
   Super groovy vendor and awesome experience overall ! I can' reiterate, the special handling on the package as it was on par with delivery and creative shipping. I can't wait to see some shrooms this vendor is offering, to get a better detail and experience once again. And much thanks to A.O.D. again !!!! :)
:)

Title: Re: AmericaOnDrugs: The Official Review Thread
Post by: yourm0m on May 20, 2013, 06:02 pm
I had typed up most of a review a few days ago whilst using the product I received from AoD, but got distracted (most likely by a shiny object) and the computer decided to reboot and dump everything I had written, so here goes my second attempt:

Product: crystal methamphetamine (.5 g)

Communication: Excellent!  The vendor replied to my first message promptly and has been very good about sending replies back and forth since.  They were willing to tailor a custom order since I was a few a dollar or two shy of having the amount needed for the .5 and really didn't want to have to go through another bitcoin transaction just for that amount.  AoD is exceptionally polite and kind, which is something not everyone values but I do, personally.  If I wanted to go get yelled at by people in the ghetto while trying to find drugs and be talked to like I am a piece of shit, I would not be paying a premium to use an internet service that requires a certain level of basic knowledge to even access, I'd be down in the ghetto overpaying for bathtub sudafed rocks with chunks of blue rock candy mixed in that the dealer claims is some real shit from Heisenberg himself.  Just kidding, that would never happen because there's no meth on the East Coast unless you find just the right gay club or trailer park, or perhaps some odd combination of the two that makes you leave feeling dirty and confused.


Stealth: Awesome.  Sealed multiple times and may even give me something to entertain myself in the future if I feel so inclined; I definitely had a genuine laugh while opening it.  I am fairly confident it would have been sufficient for international stealth, but luckily we didn't have that to worry about, which brings me to....

Shipping: Free shipping seems to be included with all of AoD's products, at least for domestic.  AoD and I had talked prior to my placing the order and they stated that despite our being on opposite ends of the US, they had every confidence that my order would arrive within 2-3 days due to priority shipping.  In the past, I have heard that before and had packages inevitably still take the usual 7-8 days, which is a long time to be waiting anxiously for some fun things.  Well, AoD said it and meant it.  My package shipped on Tuesday and arrived on Thursday.  Mind=blown.  Free priority shipping that is actually priority?  Fuck yeah!

Product (Value): I'm not sure if I'm unusual in this aspect, but the product seemed to last me FOREVER.  I stayed awake for the better part of the four days that I was constantly pretty buzzed from it (didn't try dosing between 9 PM and 6 AM generally so I could at least give my body a chance to sleep if it wanted to) and this half gram lasted.  I also shared some of it with my significant other periodically, but they are not into going hard with it like I am and staying up for days.  If I hadn't, it absolutely would have lasted me another half day.  What that translates to when running a good ol' cost/benefit analysis means that I spent $45 to have a 4.5 day-long enhancement.  I probably have a fairly high default amphetamine tolerance because I like go get crystal about once a week or every other week  lately and I had a pretty hefty adderall habit for a few months that just ended in April (probably around 200 mg every day).  So, even with those factors opposing me, I made a $45 investment last four whole days, would have been a little longer had I been stingy with my better half, but I would much rather share than do things alone.  I'm not sure about anyone else, but that investment is about the most I have EVER gotten value-wise from any drug purchase by a wide, wide margin.  I doubt that I could make a $45 investment in weed even last me 4.5 days if I wanted to stay blazed the whole time.

Product (Details): I'd also like to note that while I didn't get the change to weight the product since I dumped it right into a heavy container, it did look like a very healthy half G.  The shards were mostly rather small but that was likely from the way it was sealed for shipping; didn't have anything powdery mixed in, just varying size of shards, somewhat like looking at a snowflake really close up.  I didn't notice any change in effect whether I used the larger shards or the smaller shards at any time, so there isn't bullshit cut to worry about with the product unless it was included in the process prior to crystalization.  I would guess that I got 20 doses out of the .5 G at the VERY minimum, probably closer to 25 or 30, and tried it various ways.  The effects from oral consumption (my personal favourite) were very good, as they were for snorting too.  I decided to experiment and try it via IV, despite never having IV'ed meth before.  When doing my homework, I came across some people on forums saying they generally shoot .25 G at a time, which would be half of what I had gotten.  Needless to say, I didn't do that, I went with a smaller dose than I normally use for snorting to start, and worked my way up to a larger one than I usually use for snorting or oral, and found that the effects were pretty similar despite the dose.  I had heard before that IV methamphetamine is very intense and one of the greatest rushes, but I think I am spoiled by heroin and was expecting something like that.  I did feel an almost immediate surge of alertness when IVing and it somehow seems to be a little more clear-headed, but that might have just been my brain chemistry making me feel foggy towards the end of the run.  I have never tried smoking it and don't plan to since I have a deathly fear of dental problems and don't want to put myself in that situation.

So, there you have it.  AmericaOnDrugs is a delightful vendor with a product I definitely enjoyed and I will be ordering from them again.  In all honesty, I would be happy if AoD were the only vendor I ever had to work with on here again, but unfortunately I doubt that they can get me quaaludes or whatever other various endangered/extinct drug species I'm going to have to try just in the name of science.  Cheers to that.

         twenty minutes in and I start to feel the ecstatic of my brain sending a bunch of messages thru out my neurons (Frying brain feeling).
     My brother gets picked up and I start walking home,as I'm walking home the shrooms start to get a hold of me. Started out with heavy euphoria
and happiness. Non stop giggling and very small visuals. As I'm walking home they start hitting me harder so I decided I'd go for a longer walk. I start
To wander around my area and the visuals are getting stronger and very nice looking. I often saw visuals in plants,bushes,and the street pavement.
After one hour and 30 minutes of walking and enjoying the visuals and feeling and admiring the sky, I decided to go home. Entered my house and my parents had sit up a lit candle in the living room and were both off to sleep. As the lit candle illuminates the living room and there is a virgin Mary statue
it was kinda creepy but awesome. I get on my computer search through Tumblr for trippy psychedelic gifs. Talk to a special little someone, ended up touching myself. Orgasm was way easier to reach than usual and felt 10x better. By the time I had cummed most of my shroom euphoria and visuals    were long gone. Over all this was a very pleasant shroom trip not to intense at all, no body load really. And nice little visuals and great body high.

Title: Re: AmericaOnDrugs: The Official Review Thread
Post by: yourm0m on June 28, 2013, 02:53 am
Wow, what the fuck happened while I was gone??  Hope it gets sorted for you, AoD, for I am here to spread the joy of what I experienced from my most recent order from the AoD team.

Below is my life's story (okay, just the backstory to this order) and a review.  I will post "REVIEW TIME" directly above the review portion, should you care to have it somewhat abridged, but I'll warn you I'm a talker no matter what.

AoD knew I had a vacation coming up, I was going to Vegas, to a large music festival that I'm sure a few of you here know about and have enjoyed yourselves.  I asked AoD if they would be willing and able to create a mixed package for me so I could just have a bunch of uppers to sample from whilst out in Las Vegas, which AoD was happy to oblige, being the serviceman/woman that they always are.

Placed my order on Wednesday, thinking it'd ship here by Monday with Priority (I'm on the opposite coast from AoD, which is very unfortunate in itself, but hopefully I'll change that someday since this place sucks).  I waited around and was upset to see it hadn't come on Monday.  I checked with AoD and Nikki, who verified it was marked as delivered.  I trust AoD 100%, having dealt with them several times here and having absolutely NO issues.  The address I shipped this package to is in a type of area where it isn't possible for the package to have been left out at the door and snatched or anything of that nature.  So, sadly, my options were to hope that the post office erroneously marked it as delivered when it wasn't put on the truck until the next day, or to pray that the rental office at this particular property had the package, despite having checked there already twice and their having said there was nothing there for me.  Long story short, I checked with the rental office bright and early Tuesday morning and insisted they go through every single package and AoD had done some awesome packaging on this one and it was much larger than normal, we found it sitting around on its lonesome in the package area.  I promptly ran home to write AoD and Nikki a profuse apology for having not received it from the rental office sooner and I will henceforth be personally inspecting all packages' labels myself, should I need to check there again.

The packaging on this was phenomenal.  I wanted to cry when I saw how much AoD had paid for the Express shipping on a large parcel, which arrived on Saturday and should have been in my hands then, had the office not dropped the ball (still butthurt about that, sorry).  There were layers and layers securing my product and the outside world.  The concept of this particular one was novel and unique, I absolutely adored it!  I sadly had to destroy its exterior when trying to reach the goodness within, but it was well worth doing so.

REVIEW TIME:

Three products were received in this order from AoD: coke, meth, and MDMA.  The only product of AoD's which I have had before is the meth, and I've had it plenty of times from AoD, so my review will be sparse on that.  The other two are what I am really here to praise.

COKE: The coke arrived in one solid chunk, save for a few crumbles that rolled around elsewhere.  I read something on here about a bad batch of coke?  I don't think mine was from that and if it was, then please let me know when the good batch comes in so I can cash in my 401k and buy out the stock.  The coke was easily the best I've had in years, since maybe 2006-ish.  It wasn't fishscale in its appearance, but it had the cleanliness and taste of it.  No burn when snorting, somewhat moist and clumpy, definitely need a razor blade to get it into a fine powder.  The high from it was absolutely wonderful for coke; it did not have any kind of tweakiness or edginess at any point, even the comedown.  I find that meth has less harsh of a comedown for me (not sure whether that is odd or not), but I would happily spend money on this coke again, it was fantastic.  Again, very curious to know whether this was part of the 'bad' batch.  The high itself is very subtle, which is how I like my coke to be, rather than knocking you off your ass and melting your face while you scream at people.  It made me more sociable and just pleasant feeling without any trace of edginess.  I haven't bought coke from SR before, but I have done it hundreds if not thousands of times in my life, and this was in the top ten I have ever done, easily.  I definitely wish I had bought more for the trip!

MDMA (molly):  Again, received in one very large, brown sugar-like chunk.  The core brown pile was coated in crystaline shards, which may have been meth since the meth somehow escaped its initial hiding place in transit.  I had never done brown MDMA before (to my knowledge; I'm sure I've popped some in a club without really looking at them before), so I was very apprehensive.  I did, however, get some MDMA/MDA combination caps from vendor ForeverJung recently that had a very similar looking product within and those caps were absolutely excellent.  Due to my apprehension to try this product, I tried to find an experienced roller to sample for me the night before the first night of the festival, but to no avail.  How many of you know people that turn down free MDMA that is from a very trusted source when you only want to have them check the potency of the roll?

As it happens, I'm surrounded by absolute morons because AoD's molly blew me out of the water.  I really didn't expect a whole lot from it for whatever reason, I suppose since I had been up doing meth for a couple of days by the time I tried it Friday evening, save for only two hours of sleep that day.  Despite those conditions stacking against me, everyone who tried it (four of us total) had an absolutely excellent roll.  My better half  and I both dropped only one dose the entire evening at the festival (probably about 150 mg at the very most, maybe closer to 100-120 mg) and it lasted from 11 PM to about 4 AM as an intense but not at all unpleasant roll.  The visuals of the stages at the festival were out of this world whether you were sober or rolling, so while rolling, it was just breathtaking.  The roll gave me plenty of energy; sitting on the ground was nice, but standing and walking were not burdensome in the least.  This is the complete opposite of what I felt when trying the other kind of molly that I had for the weekend on the later nights, which I am not certain whether to attribute to product or that I had tried to roll together so soon, as I normally wait at the absolute least one week between rolls.  My friends who stayed with me were devastated that we had run out of AoD's molly and had to switch over to the other stuff we brought.  I would really like to stock up on that product while I can and I'm hoping AoD opens up shop again soon so that I can do so, I would highly recommend that anyone try the MDMA from AoD; while I can't vouch for SR coke quality, I can say with confidence that AoD's is the best molly/ecstasy product I have bought on the road, probably ever, and can be compared to SuperTrips' pills but honestly probably a little better and not overwhelming.  AoD, sorry for not having more faith in it to begin with, but you have a believer now!

Needless to say, my heart is heavy that I have almost 3 grams of the other product I had purchased on here from who was reported to be one of the best domestic vendors for MDMA at this time and I frankly don't care for their product, which when taken on the second night of the festival made all noises irritating and entirely too loud, visuals extra bright rather than just the usual intensity of ecstasy (made me feel like I was rolling in direct sunlight).  Can I get an exchange slip, please?

METH: The meth, as mentioned earlier, arrived broken up and had gotten in places it shouldn't, which please understand is not nearly as bad as it sounds.  AoD packaged this as a custom order and not their standard sealing packaging.  The three products arrived in the same box, with small dividers.  Hopefully I'm not divulging too much information and I do not wish to do so, so I will leave it at that.  The meth having gotten into the other areas is completely understandable given the way it was packaged and you do not need to worry about your product having this happen.  I did let AoD know about this and how I think it could easily be remedied, should they choose to package this way again, it's an easy fix.

The product itself is on par with other meth I have gotten from AoD and other vendors on the road.  It wasn't the absolute strongest batch, but it is by no means garbage or terrible, as I am seeing some people comment.  It was very easy to distinguish the three products from one another in the aforementioned container despite crossover, and all of the meth was crystaline and shardy, even if small shards.  There was absolutely no powder cut; the only powder was very obviously granules of the coke, the clumps were too large and on their own for it to be meth cut, not to mention damp like the coke.  The product sniffs the same as other meth I have done and has about the same potency/duration of AoD's usual, which everyone knows I am a fan of.  So, nothing new there, AoD still delivering me meth that more than gets the job done.

There you have it.  That's the story of how AoD saved Vegas.  I hope everything gets sorted for you soon, AoD team, and I thank you again for the wonderful experience (and memories..and memories somewhat hindered by drug use but no regrets there) and apologize for the bullshit with the delay on my receipt of delivery.  ::bows and exits::

Quote from: yourm0m on June 28, 2013, 02:53 am
Wow, what the fuck happened while I was gone??  Hope it gets sorted for you, AoD, for I am here to spread the joy of what I experienced from my most recent order from the AoD team.

Below is my life's story (okay, just the backstory to this order) and a review.  I will post "REVIEW TIME" directly above the review portion, should you care to have it somewhat abridged, but I'll warn you I'm a talker no matter what.

AoD knew I had a vacation coming up, I was going to Vegas, to a large music festival that I'm sure a few of you here know about and have enjoyed yourselves.  I asked AoD if they would be willing and able to create a mixed package for me so I could just have a bunch of uppers to sample from whilst out in Las Vegas, which AoD was happy to oblige, being the serviceman/woman that they always are.

Placed my order on Wednesday, thinking it'd ship here by Monday with Priority (I'm on the opposite coast from AoD, which is very unfortunate in itself, but hopefully I'll change that someday since this place sucks).  I waited around and was upset to see it hadn't come on Monday.  I checked with AoD and Nikki, who verified it was marked as delivered.  I trust AoD 100%, having dealt with them several times here and having absolutely NO issues.  The address I shipped this package to is in a type of area where it isn't possible for the package to have been left out at the door and snatched or anything of that nature.  So, sadly, my options were to hope that the post office erroneously marked it as delivered when it wasn't put on the truck until the next day, or to pray that the rental office at this particular property had the package, despite having checked there already twice and their having said there was nothing there for me.  Long story short, I checked with the rental office bright and early Tuesday morning and insisted they go through every single package and AoD had done some awesome packaging on this one and it was much larger than normal, we found it sitting around on its lonesome in the package area.  I promptly ran home to write AoD and Nikki a profuse apology for having not received it from the rental office sooner and I will henceforth be personally inspecting all packages' labels myself, should I need to check there again.

The packaging on this was phenomenal.  I wanted to cry when I saw how much AoD had paid for the Express shipping on a large parcel, which arrived on Saturday and should have been in my hands then, had the office not dropped the ball (still butthurt about that, sorry).  There were layers and layers securing my product and the outside world.  The concept of this particular one was novel and unique, I absolutely adored it!  I sadly had to destroy its exterior when trying to reach the goodness within, but it was well worth doing so.

REVIEW TIME:

Three products were received in this order from AoD: coke, meth, and MDMA.  The only product of AoD's which I have had before is the meth, and I've had it plenty of times from AoD, so my review will be sparse on that.  The other two are what I am really here to praise.

COKE: The coke arrived in one solid chunk, save for a few crumbles that rolled around elsewhere.  I read something on here about a bad batch of coke?  I don't think mine was from that and if it was, then please let me know when the good batch comes in so I can cash in my 401k and buy out the stock.  The coke was easily the best I've had in years, since maybe 2006-ish.  It wasn't fishscale in its appearance, but it had the cleanliness and taste of it.  No burn when snorting, somewhat moist and clumpy, definitely need a razor blade to get it into a fine powder.  The high from it was absolutely wonderful for coke; it did not have any kind of tweakiness or edginess at any point, even the comedown.  I find that meth has less harsh of a comedown for me (not sure whether that is odd or not), but I would happily spend money on this coke again, it was fantastic.  Again, very curious to know whether this was part of the 'bad' batch.  The high itself is very subtle, which is how I like my coke to be, rather than knocking you off your ass and melting your face while you scream at people.  It made me more sociable and just pleasant feeling without any trace of edginess.  I haven't bought coke from SR before, but I have done it hundreds if not thousands of times in my life, and this was in the top ten I have ever done, easily.  I definitely wish I had bought more for the trip!

MDMA (molly):  Again, received in one very large, brown sugar-like chunk.  The core brown pile was coated in crystaline shards, which may have been meth since the meth somehow escaped its initial hiding place in transit.  I had never done brown MDMA before (to my knowledge; I'm sure I've popped some in a club without really looking at them before), so I was very apprehensive.  I did, however, get some MDMA/MDA combination caps from vendor ForeverJung recently that had a very similar looking product within and those caps were absolutely excellent.  Due to my apprehension to try this product, I tried to find an experienced roller to sample for me the night before the first night of the festival, but to no avail.  How many of you know people that turn down free MDMA that is from a very trusted source when you only want to have them check the potency of the roll?

As it happens, I'm surrounded by absolute morons because AoD's molly blew me out of the water.  I really didn't expect a whole lot from it for whatever reason, I suppose since I had been up doing meth for a couple of days by the time I tried it Friday evening, save for only two hours of sleep that day.  Despite those conditions stacking against me, everyone who tried it (four of us total) had an absolutely excellent roll.  My better half  and I both dropped only one dose the entire evening at the festival (probably about 150 mg at the very most, maybe closer to 100-120 mg) and it lasted from 11 PM to about 4 AM as an intense but not at all unpleasant roll.  The visuals of the stages at the festival were out of this world whether you were sober or rolling, so while rolling, it was just breathtaking.  The roll gave me plenty of energy; sitting on the ground was nice, but standing and walking were not burdensome in the least.  This is the complete opposite of what I felt when trying the other kind of molly that I had for the weekend on the later nights, which I am not certain whether to attribute to product or that I had tried to roll together so soon, as I normally wait at the absolute least one week between rolls.  My friends who stayed with me were devastated that we had run out of AoD's molly and had to switch over to the other stuff we brought.  I would really like to stock up on that product while I can and I'm hoping AoD opens up shop again soon so that I can do so, I would highly recommend that anyone try the MDMA from AoD; while I can't vouch for SR coke quality, I can say with confidence that AoD's is the best molly/ecstasy product I have bought on the road, probably ever, and can be compared to SuperTrips' pills but honestly probably a little better and not overwhelming.  AoD, sorry for not having more faith in it to begin with, but you have a believer now!

Needless to say, my heart is heavy that I have almost 3 grams of the other product I had purchased on here from who was reported to be one of the best domestic vendors for MDMA at this time and I frankly don't care for their product, which when taken on the second night of the festival made all noises irritating and entirely too loud, visuals extra bright rather than just the usual intensity of ecstasy (made me feel like I was rolling in direct sunlight).  Can I get an exchange slip, please?

METH: The meth, as mentioned earlier, arrived broken up and had gotten in places it shouldn't, which please understand is not nearly as bad as it sounds.  AoD packaged this as a custom order and not their standard sealing packaging.  The three products arrived in the same box, with small dividers.  Hopefully I'm not divulging too much information and I do not wish to do so, so I will leave it at that.  The meth having gotten into the other areas is completely understandable given the way it was packaged and you do not need to worry about your product having this happen.  I did let AoD know about this and how I think it could easily be remedied, should they choose to package this way again, it's an easy fix.

The product itself is on par with other meth I have gotten from AoD and other vendors on the road.  It wasn't the absolute strongest batch, but it is by no means garbage or terrible, as I am seeing some people comment.  It was very easy to distinguish the three products from one another in the aforementioned container despite crossover, and all of the meth was crystaline and shardy, even if small shards.  There was absolutely no powder cut; the only powder was very obviously granules of the coke, the clumps were too large and on their own for it to be meth cut, not to mention damp like the coke.  The product sniffs the same as other meth I have done and has about the same potency/duration of AoD's usual, which everyone knows I am a fan of.  So, nothing new there, AoD still delivering me meth that more than gets the job done.

There you have it.  That's the story of how AoD saved Vegas.  I hope everything gets sorted for you soon, AoD team, and I thank you again for the wonderful experience (and memories..and memories somewhat hindered by drug use but no regrets there) and apologize for the bullshit with the delay on my receipt of delivery.  ::bows and exits::

Nice to see you take the time to write your own fake reviews

Post by: klemmo on September 29, 2013, 12:04 am
I just wanted to post here and say I love you, I love your products and I wish I could be a regular.

4 weeks back, I was lucky enough to be the second-placed winner in your contest, even though I live in the Netherlands, and you're a US operation.  I declined the meth as I'm a weed and psychedelics fan and the MDMA, as mailing 1/8oz to Holland seemed like taking sand to the beach. You promised me a taster of your US bud varieties as a replacement, which was very kind.

This week, I received a much better prize - a small bud of dense weed, and a jar containing some honey-coloured, smooth cannabis wax, with a lovely message assuring me I hadn't been forgotten.  I've since had a good chance to try both the weed and the wax. I'm extremely happy.

I vape most top Amsterdam varieties at home, but I've found your (unidentified) bud to be better than anything I've smoked in a month (since Starbud Sister in fact) - a full, behind the eyes stone, almost trippy.  What is it?

I have several concentrates and hashes to smoke currently including NaturalOils' Superball and some top quality shatter, but your wax is the winner of this summer for me. A super-clear head high and a huge grin is my experience with tiny dabs of this.

I just wish I had more of both. What combination of flattery, pleading and Bitcoins will persuade you to deliver here? Both the bud and the concentrate are better than I've bought in Amsterdam this year.  Thank you for both of these and also for the beautiful (and perfectly stealthy) packaging!
